***beitel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beitel.html>beitel</a> (29448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beitel.html>beitel</a></i>, equivalent to *<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">beiten</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">the causative of <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijten.html>bijten</a></span></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-el</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***beits.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beits.html>beits</a> (109250)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Beize</i>. Equivalent to a derivation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beits.html>beitsen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beits.html>beits</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beits.html>beitsen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stain <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">colourant that soaks into surface</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">buitenbeits</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bek.html>bek</a> (1339)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bec.html>bec</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:bec.html>bec</a></i>.

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hou.html>Hou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bek.html>bek</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Shut your <b><a href = vnd.unilang:trap.html>trap</a></b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bekakken</i>. The root <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kak.html>kak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:shit.html>shit</a>, crap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally associated with poshness and pretentiousness, compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kakmadam.html>kakmadam</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kouwe.html>kouwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kak.html>kak</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekend.html>bekend</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekende.html>bekende</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekenden.html>bekenden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekende.html>bekendetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An acquaintance, someone known/trusted to the person of reference, yet often less than a friend
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kennis.html>kennis</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>(<i>with the definite article: <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bekende.html>bekende</a></i>) The known, what one <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> familiar with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bekende.html>bekende</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijkt.html>lijkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meestal.html>meestal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veiliger.html>veiliger</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:saaier.html>saaier</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>known</b> usually seems safer but duller.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vertrouwde.html>vertrouwde</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bekeuring.html>bekeuring</a> (14168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bekueringe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">becoringe</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekeuren.html>bekeuren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekeuring.html>bekeuring</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekeuringen.html>bekeuringen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekeuring.html>bekeurinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">fine</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">beboeting</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boete.html>boete</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bon.html>bon</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prent.html>prent</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>the act of fining</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bekken.html>bekken</a> (13864)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">becken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bacīnum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekken.html>bekken</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekkens.html>bekkens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekken.html>bekkentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>basin, broad-shaped liquid container</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> basin, geological depression</li>
<li>pelvis, basin-shaped body region</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cymbal, two-part metallic percussion instrument</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bekkenholte</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bekkenist</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bekkenslager</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bekkenslag</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">opvangbekken</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">spaarbekken</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">stroombekken</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">waterbekken</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bek.html>bek</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekken.html>bekken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to peck (at a target)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:snap.html>snap</a>, to sneer (at someone)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sound, to feel in the mouth when sung or <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial, pejorative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kiss intensely, to French kiss</li></ol>

***bekruipen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bekruipen.html>bekruipen</a> (95397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">becrupen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruipen.html>kruipen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekruipen.html>bekruipen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to creep on/ up to, to approach and/or mount by crawling, especially stealthily
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bloedzuigers.html>bloedzuigers</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bekropen.html>bekropen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> nietsvermoedend <a href = vnd.unilang:slachtoffer.html>slachtoffer</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The leaches <b>crept on</b> their unsuspecting victim.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to steal upon, to come <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, to assail <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of <a href = vnd.unilang:feelings.html>feelings</a> and thoughts</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bekruipenis</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bekruiping</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:bekruipen.html>bekruipen</a></b>
</p>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bek.html>bek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:maw.html>maw</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:trap.html>trap</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vechten.html>vechten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>

W. Hazenberg amp; Comp., page 555.</li>
